### Components & Libraries / UI Utilities

*   [vue-shortkey (‚≠ê816)](https://github.com/iFgR/vue-shortkey) - Vue-ShortKey - plugin for Vue.js.
*   [vue-throttle-event (‚≠ê20)](https://github.com/scaccogatto/vue-throttle-event) - Throttle events based on requestAnimationFrame.
*   [vue-waypoint (‚≠ê447)](https://github.com/scaccogatto/vue-waypoint) - Waypoint component for Vue, this is the easiest way to trigger a function when you scroll.
*   [vue-clickaway (‚≠ê967)](https://github.com/simplesmiler/vue-clickaway) - Reusable clickaway directive for reusable Vue.js components.
*   [vue-scrollfire (‚≠ê26)](https://github.com/vue-comps/vue-scrollfire) - Fires an event on a specific scroll position.
*   [vue-resize-directive (‚≠ê322)](https://github.com/David-Desmaisons/Vue.resize) - Vue directive to detect resize events with deboucing and throttling capacity.
*   [v-click-outside (‚≠ê925)](https://github.com/ndelvalle/v-click-outside) - Vue directive to react on clicks outside of an element without stopping the event propagation.
*   [vue-outside-events (‚≠ê56)](https://github.com/nchutchind/vue-outside-events) - Vue 2.x directive to help a specified element listen for specific events occurring outside of itself.
*   [vue-selectable (‚≠ê69)](https://github.com/JSmith01/vue-selectable) - Vue 1.x/2.x directive to make items selectable by mouse.
*   [vue-click-helper (‚≠ê9)](https://github.com/huangshuwei/vue-click-helper) - Vue2.x directive to handle click event and dblclick event on same element.
*   [v-hotkey (‚≠ê711)](https://github.com/Dafrok/v-hotkey) - Vue 2.x directive for binding hotkeys to components.
*   [vue-resize (‚≠ê460)](https://github.com/Akryum/vue-resize) - Vue 2.x component to detect DOM elements resizing (event based/no window\.onresize)
*   [vue-observe-visibility (‚≠ê1.6k)](https://github.com/Akryum/vue-observe-visibility) - Vue 2.x directive using Intersection Observer API that detects if the element is visible (in the viewport and not hidden by CSS).
*   [v-dragged (‚≠ê95)](https://github.com/zhanziyang/v-dragged) - Vue 2.x directive plugin for drag event detection.
*   [vue-esc (‚≠ê36)](https://github.com/ianaya89/vue-esc) - Vue.js directive to add a document event listener on escape keyup.
*   [vue-global-events (‚≠ê685)](https://github.com/shentao/vue-global-events/) ‚Äì A component to handle global events (like shortcuts) using Vue‚Äôs event modifiers
*   [vue-edge-check (‚≠ê31)](https://github.com/gu-fan/vue-edge-check/) ‚Äì Check browser edge to prevent transition effect triggered oddly when swipe edge with `vue-router`
